of them properly.
Okay. So first things first here is the status column here. All right.
So this status column is basically going to be blank for whenever you have ideas. So if you have
a new ad idea, you're going to put that inside of there, right? And then whenever you decide to
actually start working on that idea, whether you do a weekly call with your team, or you're just
putting your ideas in here and then you're like, all right, this is the one that I'm going to do this
week. You're then going to change the status to working.
Okay. And then from there, there's also learning. So learning is once you actually launch the ad,
and then the final one on here is filming.
So if you are planning to film specific content, or you have an idea that you want to film here, you
can turn that status into filming, which just means like you're trying to go and get content for that
specific ad idea, which is why we have that status. And then of course we have the status of
done, which means you've actually gone through this entire process. You've marked the results
and you've marked the learnings in there, which means that this is now done.
Do not mark ads done once you launch them. Okay. You put them into learning.
So it kind of like triggers your brain that this still feels like it's active, which means you need to go

And again, we usually only do that once we set something into working. And rather than calling it
a DCT, we just have started to call it batch because it's, you know, DCTs are kind of going away.
Author is very simple.
It's like whoever the idea is, is the author. So inside of here, AI is actually the author of this
concept. So he's getting credit for it.

And then the ad concept itself is I think the thing where a lot of people get confused. A concept is
just basically it's the angle. It's the idea.
It's kind of the name of the app. And so this ad concept is called the no worry parent. All right.
The idea of this ad, as you will be able to see outlined here, and I can actually open this preview.
So we're kind of skipping a few columns here, is we're going after a specific avatar. And what
we're trying to do is we're trying to feature a parent, a mom or a dad narrating their daily struggles
with keeping their home safe for their children.
The story will revolve around how indoor air quality can be overlooked as a health risk for kids,
especially with traditional humidifiers that can, you know, actually kind of put bacteria and mold
into the air. Okay. And so this is just going to say, we're going to introduce our product as the

Okay. And so that is the ad concept. The ad concept is like the no worry parent.
I'm a parent and I don't even have to worry about, about this at all. Right. Which is no parent

And now this is super important and we found ourselves actually using awareness level more
than anything when it comes to actually optimizing ads. Now there will be times where you might
actually test a specific type of ad where you actually go three different awareness levels with your
headlines or with your visuals. That's a little bit more advanced and you don't have to really think

that deep about it.
But what we usually do is we usually try to pick a specific awareness level that we want to target
as the core idea. And so if you don't know your awareness levels, you need to understand them.
But unaware is people that don't know they have any problem or anything at all.
Problem aware is people who are aware of a problem. Solution aware is people who are aware of
solutions. They know there's ways to fix dry air.
And then there's product aware, which is people who are actually aware of humidifiers. And then
there's most aware, which is people who are actually aware of this brand. And so you have to

üßÝ Purpose:

‚úÖ Key Guidelines

‚Äúperformed‚Äù acting.‚Äã

Scaling with statics only ‚Äî no video, no UGC, just images. Actually "possible"? (As a beginner)

Context: I'm launching a new brand and I don't have any video creative yet ‚Äî no UGC, no b-roll, no testimonials on camera. What I do have is strong messaging, solid research on my avatar, and the ability to pump out a high volume of static variations across different angles, formats, and hooks.

TLDR: Can statics realistically serve as TOF acquisition creative at scale when you're starting from zero with no video ads running? Or do statics only really work as MOF/BOF retargeting once you already have video doing the heavy lifting at the top? Has anyone here actually scaled cold traffic profitably on statics alone in the early days before layering in video?

My actual question: For those who started without video ‚Äî did statics work as your primary TOF creative to get initial traction and proof of concept? Or did you find that you hit a ceiling quickly and needed video to actually scale? Not talking about long-term, just the first 30-60 days of testing to find a winning angle before investing in video production.
